<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">List of 2012 Summer Olympics medal winners</h1>			<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">
				<div id="siteSub" class="noprint">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>				<div id="contentSub"></div>

				<div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="mw-parser-output"><table class="vertical-navbox nowraplinks" style="float:right;clear:right;width:22.0em;margin:0 0 1.0em 1.0em;background:#f9f9f9;border:1px solid #aaa;padding:0.2em;border-spacing:0.4em 0;text-align:center;line-height:1.4em;font-size:88%;width: 22em"><tbody><tr><td style="padding:0.4em 0"><img alt="Olympic rings" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5c/Olympic_rings_without_rims.svg/40px-Olympic_rings_without_rims.svg.png" width="40" height="18" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5c/Olympic_rings_without_rims.svg/60px-Olympic_rings_without_rims.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5c/Olympic_rings_without_rims.svg/80px-Olympic_rings_without_rims.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="342" data-file-height="158"></td></tr><tr><td style="padding-top:0.2em;line-height:1.2em">Part of a series on</td></tr><tr><td style="padding:0 0.1em 0.4em">

<div class="plainlinks hlist navbar mini" style="float:right"><ul><li class="nv-view"><a href="/wiki/Template:2012_Summer_Olympics" title="Template:2012 Summer Olympics"><abbr title="View this template">v</abbr></a></li><li class="nv-talk"><a href="/wiki/Template_talk:2012_Summer_Olympics" title="Template talk:2012 Summer Olympics"><abbr title="Discuss this template">t</abbr></a></li><li class="nv-edit"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template:2012_Summer_Olympics&amp;action=edit"><abbr title="Edit this template">e</abbr></a></li></ul></div></div></div></td>

<p>The <a href="/wiki/2012_Summer_Olympics" title="2012 Summer Olympics">2012 Summer Olympics</a>, officially known as the Games of the XXX Olympiad, were held in <a href="/wiki/London" title="London">London</a>, <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a>, from 25 July 2012 to 12 August 2012.
</p><p>Approximately 10,500 athletes participated in 302 events in 26 sports.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup> Athletes from the <a href="/wiki/United_States_at_the_2012_Summer_Olympics" title="United States at the 2012 Summer Olympics">United States</a> won the most gold medals, with 46, and the most overall, with 103. <a href="/wiki/Michael_Phelps" title="Michael Phelps">Michael Phelps</a> and <a href="/wiki/Missy_Franklin" title="Missy Franklin">Missy Franklin</a> won the most gold medals at the games with four each. Phelps also won the greatest number of medals overall winning six in total.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2">[2]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Bahrain_at_the_2012_Summer_Olympics" title="Bahrain at the 2012 Summer Olympics">Bahrain</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Botswana_at_the_2012_Summer_Olympics" title="Botswana at the 2012 Summer Olympics">Botswana</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">[4]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Bahrain_at_the_2012_Summer_Olympics" title="Bahrain at the 2012 Summer Olympics">Bahrain</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">[5]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Botswana_at_the_2012_Summer_Olympics" title="Botswana at the 2012 Summer Olympics">Botswana</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">[6]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Cyprus_at_the_2012_Summer_Olympics" title="Cyprus at the 2012 Summer Olympics">Cyprus</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">[7]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Gabon_at_the_2012_Summer_Olympics" title="Gabon at the 2012 Summer Olympics">Gabon</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">[8]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Grenada_at_the_2012_Summer_Olympics" title="Grenada at the 2012 Summer Olympics">Grenada</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">[9]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Guatemala_at_the_2012_Summer_Olympics" title="Guatemala at the 2012 Summer Olympics">Guatemala</a><sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">[10]</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Montenegro_at_the_2012_Summer_Olympics" title="Montenegro at the 2012 Summer Olympics">Montenegro</a><sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">[11]</a></sup> each won their first Olympic medal ever, with Grenada's being gold.
</p>

<ul><li><span class="citation wikicite" id="endnote_aa"><a href="#ref_aa"><b><sup>a</sup></b></a></span>  The original winner, <a href="/wiki/Nadzeya_Ostapchuk" title="Nadzeya Ostapchuk">Nadzeya Ostapchuk</a> of <a href="/wiki/Belarus" title="Belarus">Belarus</a>, was stripped of her gold medal after failing drugs tests. The rest of the competitors were elevated by one position accordingly.</li>
<li><span class="citation wikicite" id="endnote_bb"><a href="#ref_bb"><b><sup>b</sup></b></a></span>  The original silver medalist, <a href="/wiki/Darya_Pishchalnikova" title="Darya Pishchalnikova">Darya Pishchalnikova</a> of <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a>, was stripped of her silver medal after failing drugs tests. The rest of the competitors were elevated by one position accordingly.</li>
<li><span class="citation wikicite" id="endnote_cc"><a href="#ref_cc"><b><sup>c</sup></b></a></span>  The original winner, <a href="/wiki/Tatyana_Lysenko" title="Tatyana Lysenko">Tatyana Lysenko</a> of <a href="/wiki/Rusia" title="Rusia">Rusia</a>, was stripped of her gold medal after failing drugs tests. The rest of the competitors were elevated by one position accordingly.</li></ul>
